### Contributing

Please take a quick gander at the [contribution guidelines](https://github.com/avelino/awesome-go/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md) first. Thanks to all [contributors](https://github.com/avelino/awesome-go/graphs/contributors); you rock!

#### *If you see a package or project here that is no longer maintained or is not a good fit, please submit a pull request to improve this file. Thank you!*

## Audio and Music

*Libraries for manipulating audio.*

* [EasyMIDI](https://github.com/algoGuy/EasyMIDI) - EasyMidi is a simple and reliable library for working with standard midi file (SMF). ã€ğŸŒŸStar 26ã€‘

* [flac](https://github.com/mewkiz/flac) - Native Go FLAC encoder/decoder with support for FLAC streams. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 111ã€‘

* [gaad](https://github.com/Comcast/gaad) - Native Go AAC bitstream parser. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 63ã€‘

* [go-sox](https://github.com/krig/go-sox) - libsox bindings for go. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 102ã€‘

* [go_mediainfo](https://github.com/zhulik/go_mediainfo) - libmediainfo bindings for go. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 28ã€‘

* [gosamplerate](https://github.com/dh1tw/gosamplerate) - libsamplerate bindings for go. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 9ã€‘

* [id3v2](https://github.com/bogem/id3v2) - Fast and stable ID3 parsing and writing library for Go. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 132ã€‘

* [malgo](https://github.com/gen2brain/malgo) - Mini audio library. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 90ã€‘

* [minimp3](https://github.com/tosone/minimp3) - Lightweight MP3 decoder library. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 34ã€‘

* [mix](https://github.com/go-mix/mix) - Sequence-based Go-native audio mixer for music apps. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 106ã€‘

* [mp3](https://github.com/tcolgate/mp3) - Native Go MP3 decoder. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 104ã€‘

* [music-theory](https://github.com/go-music-theory/music-theory) - Music theory models in Go. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 274ã€‘

* [Oto](https://github.com/hajimehoshi/oto) - A low-level library to play sound on multiple platforms. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 507ã€‘

* [PortAudio](https://github.com/gordonklaus/portaudio) - Go bindings for the PortAudio audio I/O library. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 331ã€‘

* [portmidi](https://github.com/rakyll/portmidi) - Go bindings for PortMidi. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 222ã€‘

* [taglib](https://github.com/wtolson/go-taglib) - Go bindings for taglib. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 72ã€‘

* [vorbis](https://github.com/mccoyst/vorbis) - "Native" Go Vorbis decoder (uses CGO, but has no dependencies). ã€ğŸŒŸStar 24ã€‘

* [waveform](https://github.com/mdlayher/waveform) - Go package capable of generating waveform images from audio streams. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 269ã€‘


## Authentication and OAuth

*Libraries for implementing authentications schemes.*

* [authboss](https://github.com/volatiletech/authboss) - Modular authentication system for the web. It tries to remove as much boilerplate and "hard things" as possible so that each time you start a new web project in Go, you can plug it in, configure, and start building your app without having to build an authentication system each time. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 2089ã€‘

* [branca](https://github.com/hako/branca) - Golang implementation of Branca Tokens. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 99ã€‘

* [casbin](https://github.com/hsluoyz/casbin) - Authorization library that supports access control models like ACL, RBAC, ABAC. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 5914ã€‘

* [cookiestxt](https://github.com/mengzhuo/cookiestxt) - provides parser of cookies.txt file format. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 2ã€‘

* [go-jose](https://github.com/square/go-jose) - Fairly complete implementation of the JOSE working group's JSON Web Token, JSON Web Signatures, and JSON Web Encryption specs. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 1441ã€‘

* [go-oauth2-server](https://github.com/RichardKnop/go-oauth2-server) - Standalone, specification-compliant,  OAuth2 server written in Golang. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 1416ã€‘

* [gologin](https://github.com/dghubble/gologin) - chainable handlers for login with OAuth1 and OAuth2 authentication providers. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 1141ã€‘

* [gorbac](https://github.com/mikespook/gorbac) - provides a lightweight role-based access control (RBAC) implementation in Golang. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 972ã€‘

* [goth](https://github.com/markbates/goth) - provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to use OAuth and OAuth2. Handles multiple providers out of the box. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 2500ã€‘

* [httpauth](https://github.com/goji/httpauth) - HTTP Authentication middleware. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 190ã€‘

* [jeff](https://github.com/abraithwaite/jeff) - Simple, flexible, secure and idiomatic web session management with pluggable backends. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 183ã€‘

* [jwt](https://github.com/robbert229/jwt) - Clean and easy to use implementation of JSON Web Tokens (JWT). ã€ğŸŒŸStar 78ã€‘

* [jwt](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/jwt) - Lightweight JSON Web Token (JWT) library. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 141ã€‘

* [jwt-auth](https://github.com/adam-hanna/jwt-auth) - JWT middleware for Golang http servers with many configuration options. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 165ã€‘

* [jwt-go](https://github.com/dgrijalva/jwt-go) - Golang implementation of JSON Web Tokens (JWT). ã€ğŸŒŸStar 6883ã€‘

* [loginsrv](https://github.com/tarent/loginsrv) - JWT login microservice with plugable backends such as OAuth2 (Github), htpasswd, osiam. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 884ã€‘

* [oauth2](https://github.com/golang/oauth2) - Successor of goauth2. Generic OAuth 2.0 package that comes with JWT, Google APIs, Compute Engine and App Engine support. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 2666ã€‘

* [osin](https://github.com/openshift/osin) - Golang OAuth2 server library. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 1576ã€‘

* [paseto](https://github.com/o1egl/paseto) - Golang implementation of Platform-Agnostic Security Tokens (PASETO). ã€ğŸŒŸStar 288ã€‘

* [permissions2](https://github.com/xyproto/permissions2) - Library for keeping track of users, login states and permissions. Uses secure cookies and bcrypt. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 382ã€‘

* [rbac](https://github.com/zpatrick/rbac) - Minimalistic RBAC package for Go applications. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 44ã€‘

* [scope](https://github.com/SonicRoshan/scope) - Easily Manage OAuth2 Scopes In Go. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 3ã€‘

* [scs](https://github.com/alexedwards/scs) - Session Manager for HTTP servers. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 656ã€‘

* [securecookie](https://github.com/chmike/securecookie) - Efficient secure cookie encoding/decoding. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 34ã€‘

* [session](https://github.com/icza/session) - Go session management for web servers (including support for Google App Engine - GAE). ã€ğŸŒŸStar 95ã€‘

* [sessiongate-go](https://github.com/f0rmiga/sessiongate-go) - Go session management using the SessionGate Redis module. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 8ã€‘

* [sessions](https://github.com/adam-hanna/sessions) - Dead simple, highly performant, highly customizable sessions service for go http servers. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 49ã€‘

* [sessionup](https://github.com/swithek/sessionup) - Simple, yet effective HTTP session management and identification package. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 76ã€‘

* [signedvalue](https://github.com/sashka/signedvalue) - Signed and timestamped strings compatible with [Tornado's](https://github.com/tornadoweb/tornado) `create_signed_value`, `decode_signed_value`, and therefore `set_secure_cookie` and `get_secure_cookie`. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 8ã€‘

## Benchmarks

* [autobench](https://github.com/davecheney/autobench) - Framework to compare the performance between different Go versions. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 90ã€‘

* [go-benchmark-app](https://github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app) - Powerful HTTP-benchmark tool mixed with Ğb, Wrk, Siege tools. Gathering statistics and various parameters for benchmarks and comparison results. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 20ã€‘

* [go-benchmarks](https://github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks) - Few miscellaneous Go microbenchmarks. Compare some language features to alternative approaches. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 130ã€‘

* [go-http-routing-benchmark](https://github.com/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark) - Go HTTP request router benchmark and comparison. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 1333ã€‘

* [go-web-framework-benchmark](https://github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark) - Go web framework benchmark. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 1101ã€‘

* [go_serialization_benchmarks](https://github.com/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks) - Benchmarks of Go serialization methods. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 945ã€‘

* [gocostmodel](https://github.com/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel) - Benchmarks of common basic operations for the Go language. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 55ã€‘

* [golang-sql-benchmark](https://github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark) - Collection of benchmarks for popular Go database/SQL utilities. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 50ã€‘

* [gospeed](https://github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed) - Go micro-benchmarks for calculating the speed of language constructs. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 100ã€‘

* [kvbench](https://github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench) - Key/Value database benchmark. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 16ã€‘

* [skynet](https://github.com/atemerev/skynet) - Skynet 1M threads microbenchmark. ã€ğŸŒŸStar 946ã€‘
